 21 |out vec4 color;
 22 |
 23 |void main() {
 24 |	// Normal en el espacio de la c炅ara
 25 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix *normal);
 26 |	// V本tice en el espacio de la c炅ara
 27 |	vec4 pos4 = vec4(position, 1.0);
 28 |	vec3 eposition=vec3(modelviewMatrix * pos4);
 29 |	// C涇culo de la iluminaci蚤
 30 |	color = max(0.0, dot(eN, normalize(lightpos-eposition))) * diffuseColor;
 31 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * pos4;
 32 |}
 33 |
Fragment shader: ../p7/p7.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |in vec4 fragColor;
  4 |
  5 |out vec4 finalColor;
  6 |
  7 |
  8 |void main() {
  9 |	finalColor = fragColor;	
 10 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
  4 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
  5 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
  6 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
  7 |
  8 |layout (triangles) in;
  9 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 10 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 11 |
 12 |in vec4 color[3];
 13 |out vec4 fragColor;
 14 |
 15 |// linalg.norm
 16 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 17 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 18 |}
 19 |
 20 |// Check if q in cylinder
 21 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 22 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 23 |	//if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 24 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 25 |		if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 26 |			return true;
 27 |		}
 28 |	}
 29 |	return false;
 30 |}
 31 |
 32 |void main() {
 33 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 34 |
 35 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 36 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 37 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius, gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 38 |			nVertIn++;
 39 |		}
 40 |	}
 41 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 42 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 43 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 44 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 45 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 46 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 47 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 48 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 49 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 50 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 51 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 52 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 53 |				fragColor = color[i];
 54 |			}
 55 |			EmitVertex();
 56 |		}
 57 |		EndPrimitive();
 58 |	}
 59 |}

  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec4 p1, vec4 p2, vec4 vec, float r, vec4 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(normalMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos, 1.0), normalMatrix * vec4(cylinderPos2, 1.0), normalMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 1.0), cylinderRadius, normalMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec4 p1, vec4 p2, vec4 vec, float r, vec4 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius, gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius, modelviewprojMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderPos, modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderPos2, modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius, gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(vec3(modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderPos), vec3(modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderPos2), vec3(modelviewprojMatrix * cylinderAxis), cylinderRadius, gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder

 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}

 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}

 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec4 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec4 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro

 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];

 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius,  vec3(modelviewMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position))) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * normalize(cylinderAxis) + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		if (point_in_cylinder(projMatrix * cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |			nVertIn++;
 48 |		}
 49 |	}
 50 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 51 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 52 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 53 |			gl_Position = gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 54 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 55 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 56 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 57 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 58 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 61 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 62 |				fragColor = color[i];
 63 |			}
 64 |			EmitVertex();
 65 |		}
 66 |		EndPrimitive();
 67 |	}
 68 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |	//vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * cylinderAxis + cylinderPos;
 43 |
 44 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 45 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 46 |		//if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 47 |		float x = gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPos
 48 |
 49 |		if (dot(x, cylinderAxis)<0) {
 50 |			nVertIn++;
 51 |		}
 52 |	}
 53 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 54 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 55 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 56 |			gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 57 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 58 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 61 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 62 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 63 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 64 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 65 |				fragColor = color[i];
 66 |			}
 67 |			EmitVertex();
 68 |		}
 69 |		EndPrimitive();
 70 |	}
 71 |}

 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}

------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec4 p1, vec4 p2, vec4 vec, float r, vec4 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |
 43 |	vec4 cylinderN = normalMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 1.0);
 44 |	vec4 cylinderPos1 = vec4(cylinderPos, 1.0);
 45 |	vec4 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * cylinderN + cylinderPos1;
 46 |
 47 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 48 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 49 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos1, cylinderPos2, cylinderN, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position)) {
 50 |			nVertIn++;
 51 |		}
 52 |	}
 53 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 54 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 55 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 56 |			gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 57 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 58 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 61 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 62 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 63 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 64 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 65 |				fragColor = color[i];
 66 |			}
 67 |			EmitVertex();
 68 |		}
 69 |		EndPrimitive();
 70 |	}
 71 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder TODO ahora mismo tiene en cuenta la posici칩n de la vista
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec4 p1, vec4 p2, vec4 vec, float r, vec4 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |
 43 |	vec4 cylinderN = normalMatrix * vec4(cylinderAxis, 1.0);
 44 |	vec4 cylinderPos1 = vec4(cylinderPos, 1.0);
 45 |	vec4 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * cylinderN + cylinderPos1;
 46 |
 47 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 48 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 49 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos1, cylinderPos2, cylinderN, cylinderRadius,  gl_in[i].gl_Position)) {
 50 |			nVertIn++;
 51 |		}
 52 |	}
 53 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 54 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 55 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 56 |			gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 57 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 58 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 59 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 60 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 61 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 62 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 63 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 64 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 65 |				fragColor = color[i];
 66 |			}
 67 |			EmitVertex();
 68 |		}
 69 |		EndPrimitive();
 70 |	}
 71 |}

Geometry shader: ../p7/p7.geom
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 13 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 14 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // direcci칩n del eje (vector unitario)
 15 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 16 |
 17 |layout (triangles) in;
 18 |layout (triangle_strip) out;
 19 |layout (max_vertices = 3) out;
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |// linalg.norm
 25 |float linalgnorm(vec3 vec) {
 26 |	return sqrt(vec[0]*vec[0]+vec[1]*vec[1]+vec[2]*vec[2]);
 27 |}
 28 |
 29 |// Check if q in cylinder
 30 |bool point_in_cylinder(vec3 p1, vec3 p2, vec3 vec, float r, vec3 q) {
 31 |	// Check that q is between the two circular faces of the cylinder
 32 |	if (dot(q-p1, p2-p1) >= 0 && dot(q-p2, p2-p1) <= 0) {
 33 |		// Check that q is inside the curved surface of the cylinder
 34 |		//if(linalgnorm(cross(q-p1, vec)) <= r * linalgnorm(vec)) {
 35 |			return true;
 36 |		//}
 37 |	}
 38 |	return false;
 39 |}
 40 |
 41 |void main() {
 42 |
 43 |	vec3 cylinderPos2 = cylinderHeight * cylinderAxis + cylinderPos;
 44 |
 45 |	int i, nVertIn = 0;
 46 |	for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 47 |		if (point_in_cylinder(cylinderPos, cylinderPos2, cylinderAxis, cylinderRadius, inverse(viewMatrix) * gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz)) {
 48 |			nVertIn++;
 49 |		}
 50 |	}
 51 |	// Si todos los vertices est치n dentro, no dibujamos el triangulo
 52 |	if (nVertIn < 3) {
 53 |		for (i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 54 |			gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 55 |			if (nVertIn == 2) {
 56 |				// Si hay dos v칠rtices dentro, se dibuja de rojo
 57 |				fragColor = vec4(0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 58 |			} else if (nVertIn == 1) {
 59 |				// Si hay un v칠rtice dentro, se dibuja de verde
 60 |				fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 61 |			} else if (nVertIn == 0) {
 62 |				// Si no hay v칠rtices dentro, no se modifica
 63 |				fragColor = color[i];
 64 |			}
 65 |			EmitVertex();
 66 |		}
 67 |		EndPrimitive();
 68 |	}
 69 |}
